The Hardware Industry in Shanghai By China Credit Editorial Board (Outline of Shanghai Industry and Commerce, No. 27) 142

2. Price Fluctuations of Hardware

The unit of measurement for hardware varies greatly due to the wide variety and different properties of the goods. These units include tons, piculs, bundles, coils, boxes, sheets, etc. Generally speaking, copper, tin, and lead are measured in piculs; steel bars are measured in tons; sheet iron, steel plates, and copper wire are mostly measured in piculs for bulk transactions and in sheets for small quantities. Tinplate is measured in boxes, wire nails are measured in bundles, and lead is measured in coils or piculs. Black sheet iron is measured in bundles or piculs. Other items, such as locks, knives, saws, hinges, and chains, are measured in dozens or grosses. Price fluctuations in the hardware manufacturing market depend on fluctuations in overseas prices. At the same time, the amount of inventory and the strength or weakness of demand are also related to market prices. However, we must also pay attention to exchange rate fluctuations. For example, after October of last year, the exchange rate plummeted, and hardware prices rose sharply accordingly, which is a clear example. As for the quoted prices in transactions, there is no standard market price, so each company often has different prices. The reasons for this are roughly four: first, the amount of each company's inventory; second, different market observations; third, small profits are made quickly; fourth, their own economic conditions. Comprehensive research on the above factors can provide clues to price fluctuations in the hardware market.

3. Current Situation of Hardware Dealers and Manufacturers in this City

The distribution of the hardware industry in this city seems to be somewhat regulated. The hardware stores on Broadway and Seward Road in Hongkou are generally small hardware businesses. The hardware stores on the west side of Tianhougong Bridge, North Suzhou Road, and the area around the intersection of Mingguo Road and Beijing Road are mostly large hardware businesses. The copper and tin industry is located in the French Concession and various locations on Mingguo Road in the southern part of the city. The iron industry is located near Toubalang on the east side of Tianhougong Bridge and various locations in the southern part of the city. Statistics from industry associations show that there are more than a hundred companies in the four industries. In terms of business affiliations, those from Ningbo are the most numerous, followed by those from Wuxi, and then other affiliations. The various situations are described below:

Organization and Capital - Hardware businesses in Shanghai are mostly partnerships, with fewer sole proprietorships, and company organizations are extremely rare. The amount of capital varies greatly depending on the business situation. Businesses dealing in copper and tin range from five or six thousand yuan to forty or fifty thousand yuan, with most ranging from five or six thousand to ten thousand yuan. Iron businesses range from a maximum of thirty or forty thousand yuan to a minimum of four or five thousand yuan, with most ranging from six or seven thousand to ten thousand yuan. Small hardware businesses range from about fifty or sixty thousand yuan at the high end to five thousand to over ten thousand yuan at the low end, with a common range of about ten to twenty thousand yuan. Large hardware businesses range from nearly twenty or thirty thousand yuan for the larger ones to around ten thousand yuan for the medium ones, and three to five thousand yuan for the smaller ones. In general, the capital of most hardware businesses in Shanghai averages from five thousand to ten thousand yuan, accounting for about seven or eight tenths of the industry in the city, with only a few companies having over fifty or sixty thousand yuan. (To be continued)

Qin Furong Accused of Obstructing Family; Ling Azhao Sues for Solace Money 143

Qin Furong, the owner of Qin Shunde Hardware Store on Mantingfang, Ma Road, a native of Wuxi, is 34 years old. He was recently sued by Ling Azhao, an 18-year-old woman from Suzhou residing at No. XX Dade Lane, Chengdu Road, through her mother Ling Zhu as her legal guardian. Attorney Li Zhendong filed a lawsuit with the First Special Court, accusing him of obstructing family and violating Articles 227 and 240 of the Criminal Law, and also filed a civil suit requesting payment of 10,000 yuan as solace money. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Huang Risheng opened court in the Eighth Criminal Division for a joint hearing. The defendant Qin Furong arrived with his defense attorneys Wu Yikun and Lu Shidao, while the plaintiff Ling Zhu and Ling Azhao did not arrive. The case was presented by the representative, Attorney Li, who stated that Ling Azhao rented the defendant's spare house, and therefore became acquainted with the defendant. Two years ago, when Azhao was not yet sixteen years old, she was taken by the defendant to a room at the Nanjing Hotel for sexual intercourse. Last year, in March, he rented a room at No. 11, 3rd floor, No. 90 Hengmao Lane, Baxianqiao, French Concession for cohabitation. At that time, Azhao's mother, Ling Zhu, was completely unaware. Later, the defendant suddenly abandoned Azhao. Ling Zhu then found a way to take her back. Therefore, based on the defendant's behavior which has violated the criminal law, they are filing a lawsuit. When questioned, Qin Furong testified that Ling Azhao's uncle, named Azeng, rented his spare house and owed four months' rent. He repeatedly demanded payment without success, so he ordered him to move out last year, resulting in a slight resentment. Azhao occasionally visited her uncle's place, so she got acquainted with him, but there was no relationship. It was found out that Azhao was a tea girl at the Wing On Company, etc. The judge, noting that the plaintiff had not arrived, ordered a retrial on the 7th of next month.

Pushan Hospital Autopsies Female Corpse After Poisoning; Reason Given Was Abuse by Male Colleague from the Same Factory 144

Shi Jiliang, a native of Shaoxing, residing at No. 40 Xinyi Lane, Chang'an Road, Zhabei, had a wife named Ma Xingzhen, 21 years old, also from Shaoxing. She worked at the Chongyang Silk Weaving Factory on Chang'an Road. Recently, Shi Ma Xingzhen had an argument with a male colleague from the factory named Yu Hegui over trivial matters, which escalated into a mutual fight. Ma, being weaker, suffered some humiliation. She was pregnant for several months and had a miscarriage. Her husband, Shi Jiliang, is a good man and did not want to cause trouble, so she had to swallow her anger. Unexpectedly, Yu Hegui, thinking Ma and others were easy to bully, invited ruffians such as Yu Zhuting and others, who arrived in ten rickshaws, to Ma's house and started a dispute with Shi Ma. As a result, Ma was forced to spend seven yuan to offer a table of food as a bribe. Five yuan was for a table of food and two yuan was for firecrackers. Afterwards, she poisoned herself because she had no outlet for her anger. Around 5 a.m. yesterday morning, her husband, Shi Jiliang, discovered her. He called the neighbors to send the young woman to Pushan Hospital on Xinmin Road for treatment. Doctor Jia Shirong examined her and found that she had taken a large amount of raw opium. The poisoning had lasted for a long time, and the poison had spread. She died before receiving treatment. The hospital reported the incident to the Xin Zha Public Security Bureau, which summoned the deceased's husband, Shi Jiliang, to inquire about the situation. Meanwhile, the local guarantor, Shen Xiaowu, reported to the Shanghai District Court and requested an autopsy. Around 3 p.m., Prosecutor Zhao Chuanjia arrived at the hospital and confirmed that the deceased Shi Ma had died of poisoning.

Letter 150

To the Editor,

Regarding yesterday's news article "News Magazine Review Committee Issued Survey Forms Yesterday," published by our agency, the statement that the committee is affiliated with the Second Section of the Public Security Bureau was a misunderstanding. The News and Magazine Review Committee is organized by the municipal government in conjunction with relevant bureaus and departments, and reports directly to the municipal government. The Public Security Bureau also sends personnel to participate in investigation work, but the committee is not affiliated with the bureau. We hope you will investigate and correct this.

Sincerely,

Jiangnan University Football Tournament: Today, Guanghua vs. Fudan; at 3 PM at Fudan Stadium; Both Teams are Well-Matched, Competition is Expected to be Fierce 153

After Jinling Central and other universities formed the Nanjing Municipal Sports Association, Jiangnan University only has Fudan, Jinan, Chi'en, and Guanghua universities left. The current sports competitions have already concluded, except for football. Since the start of the tournament last year, it has been repeatedly postponed due to various reasons, resulting in no champion yet. The teams participating for the championship are Jinan, Fudan, and Guanghua. In the first match, Jinan tied with Guanghua. In the second match, Jinan defeated Fudan. Jinan has three points, Guanghua has two points, and Fudan has zero points. Today, the third match between Guanghua and Fudan will be held at 3 PM at Fudan Stadium, with Liu Chunshu as the referee. This battle will decide Guanghua's final championship. If Guanghua loses to Fudan, then Jinan will win this year's championship, Fudan will be the runner-up, and Guanghua will be the third-place finisher. Guanghua and Fudan are evenly matched in terms of football skills, and it is expected that today's match will be a fierce competition.

John Ma Discusses World Games Track and Field Preliminaries; Emphasizes Form Over Standard Regulations; Beijing-Tianjin Inspection Team to Germany to Depart for Beijing on the 12th 154

(Beijing News) China's track and field preliminaries for the World Games will be held on the 7th at Shen Park in Shanghai. Committee Chairman John Ma is scheduled to travel to Shanghai on the 3rd to oversee everything. The reporter specially visited Mr. Ma and inquired about the athlete selection methods and objectives. According to him, he was commissioned by the National Sports Association to go to Shanghai to preside over the preliminary competition. With the selection period approaching, he decided to go to Shanghai on the 3rd to oversee everything. As for the selection methods, representative methods, and objectives, there are roughly some regulations. The selection method is only to consider the style of running or jumping and the speed and performance during the preliminary competition. The selection objective is based on individual performance. The external rumors about selecting athletes according to the track and field performance standards announced by the National Sports Association are absolutely incorrect. In addition, the age of the selected athletes and whether their future careers are suitable for long-term training and development are also important criteria. The quota is set at 12 or 16 people, but it is still difficult to determine.

The sports inspection team accompanying the Chinese delegation to the World Games to Germany is scheduled to depart from Shanghai by Italian mail ship on the 26th of this month and is expected to arrive in Berlin on July 22. On September 4, the entire team will return to China and is expected to arrive in Shanghai on September 27. The round trip will take three months. The applications recommended by the provinces and cities, as well as the sports inspectors to Germany subsidized by the National Sports Association, have been reviewed and determined. Li Zhou, the representative of Beijing, and Zhao Wenzao, the sports supervisor of Hebei Province, Xu Yanchao of the Normal University, Xia Xiang of Tsinghua University, and Li Youzhen of Luhe in Tongzhou will travel together to the Ministry of Education in Beijing on the 12th to report, and then go to Shanghai. Zhao Wenzao has returned to Baoding to handle all matters related to going to Germany, and he will come to Beijing in three or four days. The exact amount of Li Zhou's travel expenses to Germany has been set at 2,000 yuan, which has already been allocated.

Guangdong Swimming Team Organizes Water Polo Class; Begins Recruiting New Members; New Plan for This Year Drafted 159

The only swimming teams in this city organized and managed by Chinese are the Guangdong and Zhongqing swimming teams. The Guangdong team has produced many talented athletes and achieved remarkable results. Recently, the head of the team, Mr. Li Rixin, has returned to Shanghai from Hong Kong to revive the team. The various departments are working hard, and they are currently recruiting members. The team will also organize water polo training classes. Details are as follows:

Recruitment of Members: The team leader recently obtained the consent of the swimming pool management to reserve the time from 6:00 AM to 7:30 AM every morning for the team's swimming sessions. All old members of the team will continue to participate, and new members are actively being recruited. The registration period is from the 1st to the 10th of this month, at the team's new office on the third floor of No. 454 Hankou Road, from 9:00 AM to 12:00 PM and from 2:00 PM to 4:00 PM. The membership fee is six yuan, and members will enjoy full rights for the year. However, due to various limitations, the number of places is extremely limited. Team members will still be provided with special transportation as in previous years, departing from Xin at 5:45 AM every morning, passing through North Sichuan Road directly to the Municipal Swimming Pool. Detailed rules can be obtained from the team's office.

This Year's Plan: The plans made by the team last year have all been realized one by one. This year, the team will continue to promote the popularization of swimming and improve the level of swimming. High-level and beginner training will continue uninterrupted, and accommodation training will be held. Training equipment will be added to correct the movements of the hands, feet, and body, so that training is aligned with scientific methods. The team also plans to organize long-distance swimming. In addition, a water polo training class will be organized, and team members' performance will be tested weekly, focusing on strength and not being overly concerned with winning championships. The team's officers were newly elected last year, with Mr. Xu Heng as the team leader and Mr. Huang Yuexiong and Mr. Jing Ling as the deputy team leaders.

Various Schools to Celebrate Teacher's Day the Day After Tomorrow; Municipal Education Bureau Disallows Holiday; School Calendar for the 24th Year Has No Provision; In Light of the National Crisis, Work Should Be Intensified 161

The joint association of faculty and staff of large, medium, and small schools in this city recently organized the Shanghai Teacher's Day Celebration Preparatory Committee, requesting the Municipal Education Bureau to order all schools to have a day off on June 6th for Teacher's Day. However, the school calendar for the 24th year of the bureau does not provide for a holiday for Teacher's Day, and during this time of national crisis, the education sector should intensify work at all times. It was approved that Teacher's Day this year will not be a holiday, and all levels of schools will continue to have classes as usual. However, each school may select representatives or hold meetings to celebrate and commemorate.

Publishing of Special Editions: The joint association of faculty and staff of large, medium, and small schools will publish special editions in Shen Bao, Xinwen Bao, Dagong Bao, and Education Daily on this day. In addition to inscriptions by Mayor Wu and Director Pan, the content will include Jian Baizhi's proposal to celebrate Teacher's Day and promote literacy education, Chen Jicheng's article on national crisis education and teachers, Zhou Feicheng's article on the important tasks of Teacher's Day, Tai Shuangqiu's article on the review and prospect of Teacher's Day, Feng Yixian's article on the responsibilities of elementary school teachers in extraordinary times, and Sun Yucai's article on Teacher's Day and Children's Day. In addition, Hu Shuyi, Chen Gongsu, Jiang Kanghu, Xu Zexiang, Wu Zimu, Pan Dingyuan, Zhao Shusheng, and Li Ruihua will also have works published.

Separate Meetings: The joint association of faculty and staff of large, medium, and small schools in this city will hold a celebration ceremony in the auditorium for Teacher's Day. The celebration meeting of the Municipal Elementary School Faculty and Staff Joint Association was originally scheduled to be held at the Jincheng Grand Theater, but because participation was inconvenient, the location will be changed. A decision will be made this morning. The association also plans to issue a Teacher's Day declaration.

National Children's Art Exhibition to Open in This City the Day After Tomorrow; Arrangement Team Working Overnight to Display Exhibits from Various Places 162

The National Children's Painting Exhibition, organized by the National Children's Year Implementation Committee, has been completed after months of preparation. It is scheduled to open on June 6th at the Municipal Sports Field in the city center, and will last for ten days. The progress is divided into several stages.

Preparation Process: The preparatory members of the committee are Pan Gongzhan and Chen Heqin of the National Children's Year Implementation Committee, Hu Shuyi and Qian Fugong of the Municipal Education Bureau, Jiang Jianbai and Sun Yongyi of the Shanghai Municipal Children's Year Implementation Committee, Zhang Kechang and Ma Gongyu of the Chinese Art Education Society, Chen Tiesheng and Chen Zhengfan of the Chinese Child Welfare Association, and Zhou Wanghe and others of the Shanghai Children's Welfare Association, totaling ten people. A preparatory committee was established on January 20th to begin preparations and formulate various rules and regulations. The collection of entries began on February 10th and ended on May 20th, and the review of entries began. The preparation has lasted for more than five months.

Participating Units: The participation of entries from all over the country has been enthusiastic, including Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, Rehe, Shanxi, Shaanxi, Suiyuan, Henan, Nanjing, Shanghai, Qinghai, Weihaiwei, Zhejiang, Jiangxi, Hebei, Hunan, Hubei, Guangdong, Shandong, Jiangsu, Chahar, Fujian, Tianjin, Beiping, and other 24 units. There are a total of 40,000 entries, and there are also more than 2,000 entries from independent participants. 10,000 pieces have been reviewed and approved. Other works, such as works by adults and Western children, will also be displayed, numbering several thousand pieces.

Working Overnight to Arrange: Committee members of the arrangement and design committee, such as Fu Bochang, Pan Gongwang, Zhou Xibao, Ye Fengming, etc., are working very hard to arrange the exhibition due to the approaching opening. There are a total of forty exhibition rooms. The display methods used are three-dimensional, wave-shaped, three-dimensional, and tiered. Each exhibition room is decorated with harmonious colored lining paper. The special products of each province and city are symbolized with artistic patterns, making them particularly beautiful and vivid.

Painting Performance: In order to increase the interest of viewers, the conference has arranged for children's painting performances on a daily basis, where they can demonstrate their skills to guests. The participating schools and individuals include Bide, Shihua, Guangming, He'an, Daozhong, Wanzhu, Qingpu, Xixi, Songjiang, Guangqi, Minsheng, Baogong, Zhenzhong, Xintang, Mailun, Hubi, Minzhi, Wuben, Zhenjiang, Mincheng, Jiangjing, Hebei, Yinde, Yucai, Lingnan, Hankou, Jiangsu, Luhan, Guangdong Dong, Qimei, Hangzhou Provincial Girls' High School, Hangzhou Lingling Elementary School, and Guangzhou No. 1 Elementary School, as well as more than 150 independent participants. The conference has already scheduled the dates for the daily performances.

Special Editions of Various Newspapers: In order to expand publicity so that people across the country can understand the purpose of the event, the conference has published a large special edition in major newspapers across the country on the opening day. The manuscripts have already been sent out, including those for Shanghai Shen Bao, Xinwen Bao, Shishi Xinbao, Dagong Bao, Min Bao, Zhonghua Daily, Shibao, Education Daily, Hangzhou Southeast Daily, Tianjin Yongbao, Dagong Bao, Yishi, Nanjing Central Daily, Guangzhou Republic Daily, and Beiping Daily, Wuhan Daily in Hankou, and various provinces, all with inscriptions and works by educational administrators and celebrities in the education sector.

Municipal Scout Conference to Open in the City Center the Day After Tomorrow; Conference Discipline and Participation Guidelines Published 163

The 7th Municipal Scout Conference in this city is scheduled to open the day after tomorrow (the 6th) at the Municipal Sports Field in the city center. Preparations are in full swing these days. However, due to the rainy weather and the dampness of the site in front of the Municipal Government, there are problems with the camping ground. If the sun shines brightly today and tomorrow, it may still be usable. The participation guidelines and conference discipline issued by the conference preparatory committee are recorded below.

Participation Guidelines: (1) All scout troops in this city (including those that have completed registration but have not yet been issued troop numbers) must actively participate in the conference. The minimum number of participants must be 18 people. (2) Troops that have not completed registration are not allowed to participate. (3) Troops participating in the conference must be led by the troop leader or instructor. (4) The uniforms, supplies, flags, badges, and decorations of the service personnel and scouts participating in the conference must comply with the conference regulations; otherwise, they will not be allowed to participate. (5) Troops participating in the conference must fill out a report form and submit it to the conference as soon as possible for compilation. (6) All participants in the conference must participate in camping and must report and set up camp before 11:00 AM on the 6th and dismantle the camp after the closing ceremony on the afternoon of the 9th. No late arrivals are allowed. (7) Each scout and service personnel participating in the conference will be given a subsidy of 10 cents in legal tender by the conference to assist them. (8) All participants in the conference must absolutely obey orders and abide by all conference rules.

Conference Discipline: (1) Scouts and service personnel participating in the conference must abide by the scout discipline and obey the orders of the conference. (2) Scouts and service personnel participating in the conference must abide by the conference's scheduled itinerary and camp's rest times, as well as camp rules. (3) Scouts and service personnel participating in the conference must maintain the order and cleanliness of the conference venue and campsite. (4) In case of violation of any of the above, the head of conference affairs will, according to the severity of the circumstances, execute the following penalties: 1. Verbal warning; 2. Written reprimand; 3. Order to leave the venue; 4. Report to the higher authorities for punishment.

Sino-Polish Cultural Association Holds Board Meeting 168

The Sino-Polish Cultural Association held its second board meeting at its Beijing headquarters at 11 AM on the 2nd. Board members present included Chen Jianxiao, Guo Youshou, Xie Shoukang, Chu Minyi, Li Ximou, and others. Board member Chen Liuxiao chaired the meeting, reporting and resolving on various matters. A summary is recorded below: (Reports) (1) In September of last year, a tea party was held at the Beijing headquarters to bid farewell to board member Aojingsiji upon his return to his country. (2) In November of last year, the association changed its headquarters to Zhujiang Road, and then moved into a location with a monthly rent of one hundred yuan, shared with the Chinese Educational Film Association. (3) The Polish Ministry of Education established one free scholarship quota for Chinese students studying in Poland. After examination and selection by the Ministry of Education, Mr. Fang Fusen, a teaching assistant at Tsinghua University, was chosen, and a travel subsidy of eight hundred yuan was provided. Mr. Fang departed for Poland in January of this year and is currently studying road engineering at the National Warsaw University of Technology. (4) The full text of the new Polish constitution was translated into Chinese by Professor Chen Yaodong, a member of the association, and published in the March issue of the "Current Affairs Monthly." (5) The Central University Experimental School sent children's artwork and requested it be forwarded to well-known elementary schools in Poland for exchange. The association has sent it to the Warsaw Education Museum to handle. (6) The Shanghai Polish Charity Association and the association jointly organized a Sino-Polish dance party to raise funds for the education of poor Polish children and for the construction costs of the association's headquarters. The event was held on the evening of March 6th at the Paramount Ballroom in Shanghai. Many people from both Chinese and Polish social and cultural circles attended, making it a grand occasion. (7) After deducting expenses from the income of the Sino-Polish dance party, the association and the Polish Charity Association split the proceeds equally. The association received 1,314.55 yuan in national currency and deposited it in the Shanghai Bank. (8) The book "Poland: Past and Present" has been translated and will be printed after revision and the addition of new materials. (9) The association currently has 4,301.53 yuan in funds. (Discussion) (1) A proposal to edit and print a special collection of articles by association members introducing the new Polish constitution to broaden its dissemination was approved. (2) A proposal to prepare for the association's third-anniversary annual meeting was approved to be held on June 25th, and Mr. Shi Xingjia, from a Polish family famous for its motorcycles and bicycles, will be invited to attend and talk about his impressions of the industry. (3) A proposal to review new membership applications was approved, admitting Zhang Zhongdao, Fang Fusen, Guo Zixiong, Qian Ruisheng, Dan Longsheng, Xie Zhaoxiong, Zhou Shukai, Shi Zhaoying, Xie Yuanfan, Chen Lijiang, and others as members of the association.

Business News

Unabated Gold Buying Spree Drives Bid Premiums Higher 178

Settlement Prices Lower, Swap Rates Soar to $3.80

Yesterday, the gold market rose again due to foreign reports and news of the situation, which fueled buying interest among those who valued cash and foreign exchange. However, many took the opportunity to sell at the high price, leading to a gradual stabilization after a period of strength. It was observed that the overseas silver market saw a slight contraction in the London market and a flat market in the US in the morning. Floor traders claimed that after the market close, there were Indian and short-covering transactions above the listed price of 0.0625, while China was selling. Forward silver prices in Monterey contracted by one hao to one li six fen. Exchange rates were slightly longer. London spot gold fell by one penny. Reports in Japanese and Western newspapers about the situation further intensified the view of those who valued cash and foreign exchange. A large-scale buying spree appeared immediately upon market opening. The Central Bank's listed prices were announced, with the British and US currencies unchanged, and the customs gold unit unchanged. The standard bid premium price fell further to $1,131.70, but it had little impact. The off-exchange pre-market trading opened, rising to $4344, but there were few sellers. Major players such as Dadecheng, Fuxing, Yongding, and Kang all entered the market, pushing the price up to $4748. The market opened high in the morning, continuing to rise after the opening. Popular Lectures

Two Scholars of Xinhui 195

— Su Zihan

Ruan Danian was a scholar of Xinhui County, Guangdong, at the end of the Chongzhen reign of the Ming Dynasty. He was very poor and had no good clothes to wear. He ignored the ridicule of others. He was not an extraordinary figure among scholars, but he was very filial to his mother. When his mother died, he had no money to hire a mud worker, so he buried his mother himself by plastering earth. He went to her grave to cry every day, and this continued for three years.

Li Zicheng broke into Beijing, and the news that Emperor Chongzhen had hanged himself on Coal Hill reached Xinhui. Ruan Danian cried bitterly for several days and did not eat or drink for days. Then he had a thought: "It is not worth dying like this; I will die when it is worth dying!" So he resumed eating and drinking.

At that time, someone said to Ruan Danian: "I heard that when the rebel Yan entered the capital, many ministers surrendered and are still high officials. Why don't you go? Why suffer here?"

Ruan Danian sighed, "These people have no conscience. I only want to die!"

Ruan Danian did not want to die for a while because he wanted to do his best to restore the Ming Dynasty. When he heard someone advising him to surrender to the rebels, he became even more angry and immediately gathered his neighbors, wanting to start an uprising in Xinhui. But those people were too timid and had no loyalty, and no one would do it. Ruan Danian worked hard for several days with no result. He was extremely angry and sailed a small boat to Yamen. He went ashore to the Temple of Empress Yang, knelt on the ground, and cried loudly. The fishermen living on the coast of Yamen heard someone crying in the temple and ran to see. Seeing Ruan Danian crying so sadly, some people unconsciously shed tears, and some people went to advise Ruan Danian.

Ruan Danian stopped crying when he was hoarse, stood up, and saw that these fishermen were so easily moved. He felt it was an opportunity and could not let it pass easily. He said to the fishermen, "Do you know that the Emperor has been killed by the rebel?"

The fishermen were surprised and said, "We don't know. Who is this rebel?"

Ruan Danian said, "The rebel is named Li Zicheng, and he is a great robber. He rapes, kills, and burns everywhere, and has killed countless people. He has already broken into the capital and forced the Emperor to death. We are people of the Great Ming and should avenge the Emperor. Those officials only know how to make money. If we want to kill the rebels and take revenge, we must rely on ourselves. My strength alone is too small to accomplish anything. You are all people of the Great Ming, all loyal and righteous people. Let us unite and kill the rebels!"

Ruan Danian became more and more impassioned, and the fishermen also became angry, all clenching their fists and wanting to go immediately. Ruan Danian came out and quietly observed the fishermen, noticing several spirited young men. He told them what to do and then, after a few days, they agreed on a date to gather by the sea. There were one hundred and ten fishing boats and more than four hundred strong men. Ruan Danian used military tactics to organize them and set the date for the uprising for the next day.

At the same time, there was another scholar in Xinhui named Li Zichu. He was very rich, and whenever there was a bad harvest, he would take out his own money to help the poor, so many people were grateful for his kindness. When he heard the news of Chongzhen's death, he wrote a "Great Bamboo Emperor" memorial tablet, placed it in the family temple, and led his family to offer sacrifices and cry. Like Ruan Danian crying at the Temple of Empress Yang in Yamen, many people came to watch.

After Li Zichu finished crying, he stood up and said to everyone: "The Great Ming has been in power for three hundred years since Emperor Gao pacified the world. Our ancestors have received many benefits from the country for generations. Now the rebel has forced the Emperor to death. The ministers usually only know how to play around, and when there is a crisis, they surrender to the rebels, bringing the country to this point. If we, the people, do not unite to save the country, we will only go to hell day by day. We live as people of the Great Ming, and we die as ghosts of the Great Ming. Isn't that the right thing to do? But we must die worthily. Let us all find a place where it is worth dying!"

Before Li Zichu could finish speaking, a burly man in his thirties jumped out of the crowd and shouted, "If Mr. Li wants to save the country, we are willing to follow him, through fire and water together. Whoever changes his mind halfway is not born of human parents!"

Li Zichu said: "These are my good friends and good people of the country. Among our relatives and friends, there are still many loyal and righteous people. Please ask everyone to persuade them. The more people, the better."

In just over ten days, he got more than five hundred people. Li Zichu used all sorts of words of loyalty and righteousness to persuade the bandits in Xinhui County, and the bandits agreed to join the cause of saving the country. This brought the total to more than one thousand six hundred people.

Li Zichu heard that Ruan Danian was in Yamen and brought these more than one thousand people to Yamen.

These two scholars, filled with loyalty and righteousness, met in Yamen, and when they met, they embraced each other and cried loudly. The soldiers in the army were overwhelmed with emotion and wished they could kill the rebels immediately.

Ruan Danian stopped crying first and said to Brother Li: "The ministers have acted recklessly and ruined the country. Our wise Emperor also died at their hands. The country has reached this point. Fortunately, the hearts of the people have not died. You and I are just scholars, but with a call to arms, we have gathered so many loyal and righteous people. There is still hope for the country!"

Li Zichu also stopped crying and said, "Yes! The hearts of the people have not died, and the country can still be restored. Now that two emperors have already been established in the two capitals, we should still go to Nanjing to persuade the King; that is better than here."

The two asked everyone what they thought, and everyone was willing to go to Nanjing.

Ruan Danian and Li Zichu led these more than one thousand people onto boats, planning to go to sea to Shanghai, and then up the Yangtze River to Nanjing.

One day, a great wind rose at sea, and the waves, following the wind, rose and fell like mountains, rolling back and forth. Ruan Danian and Li Zichu's fleet of boats were drilling in and out, losing contact with each other. The wind blew harder and harder, and the waves grew bigger and bigger. How could these wooden boats withstand such a storm? They struggled against the wind with all their might, but it was no use. Many boats had already been overturned by the waves, and the bottoms of the boats were like upturned watermelon rinds, floating back and forth in the vast sea. The sea was full of corpses, floating there with the waves.

Although many boats had capsized, Ruan Danian and Li Zichu still struggled desperately against the storm, trying their best to keep their boats from capsizing in the mountain of waves.

The wind blew for a day and a night before it gradually stopped, and the waves subsided. Ruan Danian and Li Zichu collected the boats that had not capsized, and when they counted, they had already lost more than half, leaving only three to five hundred people. But they were still not discouraged and still led these people towards Nanjing.

That day, they reached Chongming Island and knew that they had arrived at the Yangtze River, but they also learned that Shi Kefa had died and Nanjing had fallen. The remaining three to five hundred people heard this news and knew that the situation was over. Some scattered, leaving only a few dozen people. Ruan Danian and Li Zichu had no choice but to dismiss these dozens of people and return to Xinhui.

Soon, emperors were established in Fujian and Zhejiang, but Ruan Danian and Li Zichu decided to go to Ganzhou.

When they were about to leave, everyone advised them: "Now that the rebel has died and the Qing Dynasty has occupied most of the country, what can Li Suiqiu accomplish alone? Why go!" The two did not listen and still went to Ganzhou.

When they arrived in Ganzhou and met Li Suiqiu, Li Suiqiu asked, "Why have you two come to see me? What can I do for you?"

Ruan Danian and Li Zichu answered in unison: "We have come to the General to find a place where it is worth dying."

Soon, the Qing army arrived in Ganzhou and attacked day and night without rest. Thanks to Li Suiqiu's desperate support, he held out for a few days. But the Qing army's momentum was too strong, and eventually they could not hold out. The city was broken, and the Qing soldiers poured into the city like a tide. Li Suiqiu fought the Qing soldiers in street battles, exhausted his strength, and died in battle!

Ruan Danian and Li Zichu saw the city fall and Li Suiqiu die in battle from the city wall. They drew the short knives from their sides and shouted to the sky, "Ancestors in heaven, your little servants have the opportunity to repay the country today, and it is worth dying!" The two flew down the city and stabbed the Qing soldiers, who were like a tide, killing several in a row. The Qing soldiers were initially surprised, but then saw that they were two scholars and did not take them seriously. They raised their knives and spears together, and in an instant, Ruan Danian and Li Zichu were chopped into mincemeat under the chaos of knives and spears.

Alfred Nobel 1833-1896 — Inventor of Dynamite 196

— (Guo Xuan)

Isn't everyone afraid of modern warfare? What was it that flattened Zhabei in Shanghai? Why do we feel uneasy whenever we hear a buzzing sound overhead? Why are we afraid of others and afraid to compete with them?

I think what we fear are their powerful weapons, the weapons we don't have!

These are not the days of broadswords and spears. A sixteen-inch cannon can fire a ton (over sixteen hundred catties!) of shells, and within seven miles (about thirty li), it can penetrate a foot of steel plate. What kind of person can withstand this? What kind of house can withstand this? During the European War, German soldiers forcibly passed through Belgium to attack France. The Belgians built extremely sturdy fortresses in Antwerp, budgeting for three months of defense. Unexpectedly, within eleven days, all the solid stones on the fortresses were turned into dust by German cannons, and the city had to surrender! What about airplanes? Isn't it the same? Large bombs generally weigh a ton. When that thing falls from the sky, it's like the sky is falling and the earth is splitting! A 240-pound bomb already amazes us with its power – I'm afraid even ordinary cellars can't withstand its force! – Let alone one weighing over a thousand catties!

What gives it such great power? – It's dynamite!

Speaking of dynamite, we are ashamed. This thing was invented by us Chinese! It is said that during the Sui Dynasty in China (about 1500 years ago), gunpowder was already known for performing magic tricks. By the Song Dynasty, it was used in warfare. But even now, we are still only using the charcoal gunpowder in "firecrackers" and "firework boxes," and there has been no progress. Westerners, however, have taken it and are bullying us! When we celebrate the New Year with firecrackers, have we ever thought that this thing contains so much potential?

The reason why gunpowder can generate great force is simple: it is originally a liquid or solid, but when subjected to force, electricity, or impact, it suddenly turns into a gas, and its volume increases many times over. For example, if you put some gunpowder in a house, it can blow open the windows and break the doors once it explodes. Imagine how powerful it would be if it were confined in a small gun barrel! Modern gunpowder is much more powerful than ancient gunpowder, because modern chemistry is developing faster and faster, and people know how to choose raw materials with greater explosive power to make gunpowder. The Nobel I want to talk about is the one who improved gunpowder and increased its power.

Originally, gunpowder was not only used for killing people, but it could also be used for beneficial human endeavors such as mining and road construction. For example, when a train encounters a mountain and needs to build a tunnel, how could it be done with manpower alone? At this time, a large amount of dynamite must be used. For example, the Mont Cenis Tunnel between France and Italy began work in 1857. At first, old black powder was used for blasting, and it was estimated that it would take 24 years to complete. Later, a powerful explosive was invented, and the project was completed eleven years ahead of schedule. You see, isn't dynamite also a way to benefit mankind? It just depends on how humans use it.

Nobel was from Sweden, a cold country in Northern Europe. The people of this country mostly possess strong and resilient characters, and Nobel was no exception. His father was a mechanic, so his family environment could be said to be close to science from an early age. But his father did not intend to make him a gunpowder inventor, but wanted him to continue his own career. Therefore, after graduating from middle school, he was sent to the Faculty of Engineering at St. Petersburg University in the Russian capital to study mechanics. Nobel graduated from university at the age of twenty-two.

At this time, a French Brigadier General named Picquet was very famous for his research on explosives. Picquet was originally an arms manufacturer, and he wanted to find a way to increase the firing range of bullets, so he studied improving gunpowder. Originally, the composition of early gunpowder was nothing more than a mixture of charcoal, saltpeter, sulfur, and other things. Although it could explode, the power was very small. After the news of Picquet's research on gunpowder spread in the newspapers, it aroused Nobel's interest. Because when he was in college, he had already begun to pay attention to the research of nitroglycerin, a raw material for making new explosives.

But Nobel's motivation for studying explosives was not to help humans fight wars, but to stand on the position of helping humans build. He stayed in the laboratory day and night, trying to realize his ideal. His parents did not approve of his intense actions, and many relatives and friends advised him. Some even thought that he was pursuing a shadowless dream. We can say that Nobel, like other inventors, encountered many setbacks at first. But he was not discouraged. Every day, he faced those extremely strong chemicals, such as nitric acid, sulfuric acid, etc. His clothes were burned with large and small holes, and sometimes his skin was scorched. Naturally, before his invention was successful, everyone's ridicule of him only became more and more severe.

Nobel buried himself in hard work in the laboratory, and two or three years passed in an instant. He was so tired that he was as thin as a rake and his spirit was withered, but there was still no solution to what he hoped for. Sometimes he worked until midnight alone, accompanied only by the cold moonlight. Everyone else was sleeping sweetly. When this great scientist saw his desolate situation, he couldn't help but shed a few tears.

He believed that "nitroglycerin" must have extremely violent explosive properties and could be made into a powerful explosive, but he failed hundreds of times. Later, he realized that it was not the problem of nitroglycerin, but the imperfection of the fuse. So he tried to improve the fuse again, which took him a long time, and the result was also a failure. He then improved the fuse into a detonator, spending a lot of effort, but still to no avail! He was a bit confused.

Finally, he thought of using a chemical called mercury fulminate and putting it into the detonator, which might be effective, so he began to install it. But when would it ignite? After ignition, would it really explode? He was still doubting himself when suddenly, bang, bang, bang, bang, a world-shattering sound came from in front of him! Everything he had been experimenting with flew out of the house! All that was visible was a white fog.

When the family heard the loud noise, they knew that something had gone wrong. When they came out to take a look, they saw black smoke coming from Nobel's laboratory. The roof of the house was gone, and many sundries were scattered on the ground, emitting burning smoke. His parents rushed inside, regardless of their own lives, and only then did they pull Nobel out, covered in blood. Everyone was shocked to see his pitiful appearance! But Nobel said calmly: "Don't be afraid! I won't die! ... Ah! My work is successful! Successful! ... Quick, give me a glass of water, I'm so thirsty!" Someone immediately poured him water. After he drank it, his spirits rose even more. His two hands, filled with blood, danced involuntarily. He was like a madman, spinning and dancing around the house, yelling; it turned out that he had been locked in this room for a full six years! (This was already 1864)

Nobel's nitroglycerin gunpowder was invented, and the whole world was shaken, because this thing's explosive power was many times greater than that of old gunpowder! The Swedish government specially granted him a manufacturing patent, and he received special protection from the governments of Britain, Germany, and France. Thus, Nobel's assets accumulated day by day, and the world's great projects saved countless time and effort. Who in the world doesn't praise his contribution!

But nitroglycerin is a liquid, which is extremely inconvenient and dangerous to transport. Nobel spent a lot of thought and solved this problem again. He mixed "kieselguhr" with nitroglycerin to form a soft substance, which is the famous military "dynamite." Later, he invented nitrocellulose, which is made by soaking cotton in nitric acid. It is a gelatinous substance, and its explosive power is much greater than that of dynamite, so it is also called "blasting gelatin" (this was in 1878). This also obtained a government-granted patent.

Since Nobel's invention of gunpowder, the industrial demand has become more and more frequent. In 1867, he only produced eleven tons, but in 1870, it increased to 420 tons. In 1877, it was 5,500 tons, and in 1882, it reached tens of thousands of tons. Nobel naturally made a fortune and became a world-renowned scientist. But there was one thing that caused him great pain, that is, the gunpowder that was originally intended to benefit mankind was gradually being used in self-destructive wars! Countries were all trying to manufacture gunpowder, and weapons were also being improved. In short, the methods of killing people were faster, more economical, and more cruel! This was not Nobel's original intention at all! When he was on his deathbed, he regretted his sins very much. He had eighteen million yuan in inheritance, and in order to atone for his sins, he donated all of it to the country to organize a Nobel Foundation to manage it. The annual interest earned is awarded to people from all countries who have made contributions to physics, chemistry, physiology, or literature. In addition, people who are committed to reducing armaments and world peace are also eligible for awards. Each category is limited to one person per year, and they can receive about 80,000 yuan. This is the world-renowned Nobel Prize.

Nobel lived to be sixty-three years old and died with endless regrets!

Publishing World

A Major Revolution in the Publishing World 197

— Du Xiu

—Standardize Book Prices Nationwide—

The publishing world, on the one hand, is to maintain the livelihood of a part of the people, and at the same time, it undertakes a department. Originally, it can be explained by the eight characters of "I am for everyone, everyone is for me," but in terms of comparability, there is indeed a difference in urgency and importance. For example, in the publishing world, it not only has the obligation to pass on the talents and knowledge of the predecessors to the present and the future, but also can promote the progress of this era and promote the upward development of this culture!

At the same time, in every department of this present society, there are unreasonable phenomena. This unreasonable phenomenon may bring a little benefit to a small number of people in a certain department, but it is a poison to the public. This situation is prevalent in every place and every profession line in this world. The publishing world is certainly no exception.

Only the publishing world has too profound an impact on the people, only the mission undertaken by the publishing world is too important, therefore, we demand that the publishing world eliminate its unreasonable phenomena, and it is becoming more urgent. The Ministry of Education's order to the national publishing world to standardize the catalog of books is probably here, and the Shanghai Book Industry Association first obeyed the order to do so, probably also.

In the past, publishers often set the price of books very high, and the discounts were also very large. Therefore, in the recent economic downturn, books with 20% discounts have emerged endlessly. The operators of books can be said to have lost their business ethics, and the buyers of books, of course, are deceived. Therefore, the sluggish sales of books and the pie button of culture are also expected.

It is now scheduled to start on July 1 of this year. All books will be printed with the actual price, and there will be certain regulations for low-priced pre-orders. From now on, all bookstores can reduce many unnecessary competitions, improve commercial ethics, and earnestly serve the culture, and the general readers will not be deceived.

The author firmly believes that this unprecedented major change in the publishing world is the prelude to the brilliant start of the entire Chinese cultural world!

The Problems of Kang, Tibet, Yunnan, and Guangxi in the Future 198

— Wu Qiyun

Written by Fang Qiudong, World Publishing

In the preface of Mr. Fang Qiuwei's book "The Problems of Kang, Tibet, Yunnan, and Guangxi in the Future," we read the following painful confession: "Before the September 18th Incident, I tried to write about the Northeast problem, but no one paid attention to it; after the September 18th Incident, I tried to write about the North China problem, and similarly, very few people paid attention to it; on the contrary, it was the Japanese who paid attention to my writing..." A researcher with relatively excellent vision, his labor cannot get the attention of the general public, but is paid attention to and researched by the friendly country of Japan. This is really the greatest sadness!

Now, Mr. Fang Qiuwei's book "The Problems of Kang, Tibet, Yunnan, and Guangxi in the Future" has been completed again. Assuming that the book still does not get the attention of the Chinese people, but is used as a reference by countries such as Britain, France, Japan, and Russia, then if it continues to be so confused forever, the Northeast has already been lost in the past, and the Southwest problem may follow. What else can be said about the sinking of China? Then the sadness of the author alone is just a trivial matter!

In Chinese history, the border provinces have always adopted a policy of appeasement. As long as they do not rebel, do not make trouble, and do not resist, and achieve the so-called "coming to court every year and paying tribute every year," they will be satisfied. This policy was originally not too critical in the era of closure, because with the vast territory of China, the underdevelopment of transportation, the lack of education, the differences in folk customs, and the differences in ethnic characters, it was not realistic to hope that the power of the central government would directly reach the remote provinces. However, this bad policy of appeasement is okay as a temporary expedient, but not as an unchanging policy for all ages; it is okay in the era of closed-door self-preservation, but it is not okay now. The reason why Kang, Tibet, Yunnan, and Guangxi are full of the power of countries such as Britain and France is because the central government of our country has always adhered to the policy of appeasement. (To be continued)

Political Systems of Various Countries 199

— Zhang Tianyou

Edited by Yang Youjiong and Fu Biao, China Publishing

Man is a political animal. This saying, from the establishment of the country to the infinite future, the author dares to assert that it will never shake its firmly established conclusion. Because prestige is always a person in a society, it is impossible to live in isolation and satisfy one's own life requirements. Because life requires the division of labor and cooperation of the public, the country is established, and politics is produced. So whether you like politics or hate politics, this political system is always affecting the general public; these political laws are always dominating the general public. For thousands of years in our country, in the era of monarchical autocracy, the general self-history Qinggao people often regarded not asking about politics as transcendence, but how could these hermits who hated politics escape the domination of national laws and political systems? It is the most ridiculous thing to be ruled by the political system and regard not asking about politics as Qinggao. Until the early Republic of China, Mr. Wang Jingwei once put forward the so-called Three No's Doctrine, one of the "Three No's" is not to be an official. The reason why Mr. Wang did not want to be a citizen was nothing more than to show Qinggao. However, if you do not become an official, the warlords of the Yuan Shikai family will become officials. As a result, because of the lawlessness of the rulers, there will still be a Yuan-seeking movement. In the Republic of China in the seventeenth year, Mr. Wang only became an official; here, it must be specially explained that the author's so-called interfering in politics does not mean that you must be an official to interfere in politics; and the so-called not being an official by the general Qinggao people in the past includes the entire meaning of not interfering in politics, so the author believes that Mr. Wang's slogan of "not being an official" in the early Republic of China, which includes the entire meaning of "not interfering in politics," has room for discussion. There is also our Dr. Hu Shi, who initially believed that interfering in politics was not Qinggao, but as a result, he said: "I want to escape politics, but politics is always following me, not letting go." (The general idea is like this, I don't remember the original text.) In the past two or three years, Mr. Hu Shi's political essays have been published from time to time, which shows that people are ultimately social animals and political animals!

In the past, the author believes that the strange phenomenon of hating politics can be explained in the following three points: First, the power of government and the power of governance were completely in the hands of the emperor alone. The emperor's words were the law and the order, and the people were not allowed to interfere; second, the wind of competition, corruption, meanness, and filth on the road to officialdom made the general self-respecting people discouraged, so they were unwilling to ask about politics; third, the relationship between the government and the people at that time was very shallow. In addition to the obligation to pay grain and taxes, the good and bad of politics had little to do with the general law-abiding and self-respecting people. The so-called "the sky is high and the emperor is far away," who can control who?

But now, social life is becoming more and more complex, economic development is becoming more and more strict, the level of education is becoming more and more universal and improved, and the idea of civil rights has reached the ends of the earth. The relationship between politics and the people is certainly not as shallow as in the past autocratic era. Therefore, the general public is concerned about politics and intervenes in politics, just like daily clothing.

After checking the second half of this article, it has been completely published in the previous issue of this publication. The front and back are reversed by the hand people. Please forgive the readers. (Editor's Note)

Supplement to Shen Bao This Port

A Difficult Problem in the League of Nations 200

— Jing

The difficult problems that are now gathered in front of us are ten times or a hundred times greater than the League of Nations, but we put them aside and do not talk about them, and go to talk about the difficult problems of the League of Nations that are completely irrelevant, to talk about how he is? No, we also thought that this League of Nations was a "big Bodhisattva who always responds to requests." Since the September 18th Incident, we have also gone to ask for advice and beg for help, but in the end, it is like drawing a lottery in the Red Temple, drawing a low lottery. In addition, we absolutely cannot get any influence.

In the September 18th Incident, we had already recognized the League of Nations for the first time. In the Italy-Abyssinia War, Abyssinia also went to "draw a lottery" in the same way. In the end, "only sincerity is spirit," and we actually drew a top lottery, getting a lot of comfort and face, but Abyssinia was finally destroyed, and the Abyssinian king also fled. This is our second time to recognize the League of Nations. The current difficult problem of the League of Nations is not other, but the aftermath of the Italian invasion of Abyssinia. Although it is the aftermath, it is indeed very difficult to deal with this problem. What is the problem? That is, the sanctions against Italy should be lifted.

When the Italy-Abyssinia war broke out, the League of Nations immediately decided to recognize Italy as an aggressor country and decided that sanctions should be imposed on Italy and implement measures. Now that Abyssinia is dead and Italy has announced Abyssinia as an Italian colony, the difficult problem of the League of Nations lies here. Should we continue to impose sanctions? I am afraid that it will cause future disputes. Should we lift the sanctions? In terms of the face of the League of Nations, it is also unreasonable. This problem does require research. It is indeed a pain that "it is difficult for me to be a person on the left and right."

The League of Nations cannot solve this problem, and it originally wanted to delay it, but Argentina, which likes to joke, suddenly asked the League of Nations to convene a conference earlier. The Argentine government originally had close relations with Italy, so Argentina was not enthusiastic when the League of Nations decided to sanction Italy. Therefore, the current request for the League of Nations to convene a conference earlier is also to help Italy, or it is said that it was indirectly initiated by Italy, and it is also credible that it will take the opportunity to urge the cancellation of sanctions in the future. On the one hand, Italy used propaganda methods, saying that if the current sanctions measures cannot be lifted before June 15, Italy should withdraw from the League of Nations. On the other hand, Italian Ambassador to the UK Grandi visited Foreign Secretary Eden to do preliminary work to ease the relations between the two countries. One hard and one soft, threat and lure, the two are advancing in parallel, which is a good diplomatic method.

However, what about the United Kingdom? If we want to be tough to the end, on the one hand, we are afraid that the League of Nations will die here and cannot be maintained. On the other hand, we are afraid of causing trouble, which is no small matter. It is really impossible to be tough. Therefore, there is indeed a possibility of understanding between the two countries, that is, the problem of canceling sanctions measures can also be solved. As for the solution path? According to the British Observer, it is only necessary to modify the agreement established between the United Kingdom and Italy in December 1925, (the agreement stipulates that the Lake Tana area in western Abyssinia is within the sphere of influence of the United Kingdom,) and replace the words of the Emperor of Abyssinia in the agreement with the words of the Italian government. In other words, the British government only needs to have the right of transfer that it requires, and the Italian government will voluntarily give it to the United Kingdom.

If we look at this piece of news, the United Kingdom only needs to obtain the area around Lake Tana in western Abyssinia as the sphere of influence of the United Kingdom, and it can lift the sanctions. If so, the United Kingdom used to help Abyssinia, but it turned out to be helping itself. As long as it gets the rights and protects the rights, the other faces can also be abandoned. The League of Nations that I used to know only thought that it was "the League of Nations is useless." The League of Nations that I now know is actually a "spoils-sharing" League of Nations. In the future, small and weak countries must realize that they must strive for self-improvement and strive for self-salvation. The League of Nations is originally a decoration in the world, and it is a black yamen in a dark mass.

The Story of a Horse 201

— Xia Lisi

That year, I was wandering around the Malay Peninsula. From one metropolis to another, sometimes even getting a meal was a problem, so I endured hunger on the streets. One day, I was so hungry that I couldn't bear it any longer. On the street, I kept looking greedily at the doorways of every food store. That sly and despicable Indian Ah Sam began to notice me, following me relentlessly. So, I crossed the bridge over the small slope, went to the wilderness with a frightened heart, wiped the sweat from my forehead, calmed down, and lay down on a patch of grass.

The sun was bright, piercing my eyes. I was exhausted, but I couldn't fall asleep. I lay there for a while, and then a horse came, grazing not far from me with its head down. The surroundings were very quiet, and the sound of it chewing grass could be heard clearly. Because of this, I was once again threatened with having nothing to eat one day. So I sat there silently watching the horse. It was very strong and must be well-nourished. Somehow, I felt a touch of envy toward it. At this moment, two people came rushing from afar, obviously looking for their horse. When they discovered it was here, they shouted with joy:

"It's here!"

For some reason, they suddenly showed me their kindness. Maybe they thought I was guarding the horse for them? Seeing my hungry appearance, they took me and the horse away together. Not far from this grassland, their stable could be seen. From their conversation, I understood that this horse was in training and would definitely participate in the big race on the Malay Peninsula in three months. Along the way, they talked about various aspects of the horse, and then suddenly asked if I wanted a job. In my state of hunger and cold, how could I refuse? So, the next day, I became a small errand boy in the stable.

Among the dozen or so horses, I always had a slight fondness for the horse I met on the grassland. Its name was Napoleon. Every morning, I led Napoleon outside for a stroll, letting the morning breeze blow on it and the sun shine on it. When it was happy, it would stretch its neck and whinny, its brown hair flowing to both sides, showing a kind of majestic air. One day, the owner saw it and laughed so hard that he couldn't close his mouth, exclaiming:

"Napoleon, you're really something!"

The owner was a British devil, with the demeanor of a gentleman, holding a walking stick and a telescope around his neck. As the race drew near, he took Napoleon to the racetrack and had the jockey run for him to see. Then he took out his stopwatch and watched very carefully. As soon as the gun went off, Napoleon ran forward, its hooves kicking up dust, making a clattering sound as it sped around the field. Everyone was very tense at this time, and even though the owner was very satisfied after it finished running, he still kept grumbling, telling us to take good care of it and intensify the training. At the same time, he introduced Napoleon in the newspapers, exaggerating that Napoleon would surely dominate this year!

In two days, it would be the day of the race. That night, it was very hot and stuffy at first. Then, in the middle of the night, a torrential rain began to fall. After watching Napoleon settle down, I closed my eyes to rest in a corner of the stable. I even had a dream, dreaming that Napoleon won first place in the Malay Peninsula race, and 100,000 people cheered for it! But when I woke up, what...

Napoleon was gone!

It had been stolen. Because those people feared that Napoleon would win their championship in the race, they did such a thing. Our owner just kept biting on his cigar, but didn't light it. After biting the cigar to pieces, he spat a mouthful of phlegm into the spittoon. He also called the police station: "You must find Napoleon within twenty-four hours!" he sternly ordered.

Naturally, I was kicked out of the stable that day. The life of wandering and starving returned, but I missed Napoleon. On the day of the race, I specially went to the racetrack crowded with thousands and thousands of people, wanting to know about Napoleon's news. But my ragged appearance aroused the interference of the Indian Ah Sam again, not allowing me to approach the entrance. Thus, in the midst of the deafening shouts, I stood outside and eagerly asked a person:

"Sir, is Napoleon running?"

"No! Washington got first place." That was his reply.

Page 20

A Day in a Cigarette Factory 202

— Ye Lai

At seven o'clock, the sun had already climbed into our dormitory. Looking out from the steel window, I could see a distant corner, and the tall chimney stood out vividly before my eyes. Many factories were sounding their whistles, wuwu—this sound was already urging me. I quickly washed my face. The oily substance stuck to my yellow-black face was strangely sticky, and it was hard to wash it clean. However, in this cigarette factory, I was immersed in an atmosphere of tobacco mixed with hemp wine all day and night. Although I am not a person who smokes cigarettes, I have become like a demon stained with the smell of tobacco.

It wasn't time to start work yet. In fact, it wouldn't be officially work time until nine o'clock. What should I do? I am a very unfamiliar clerk. So, I ran around the huge factory like an inspector. However, I really like to go to various departments to observe in the morning, especially before work starts, when there is plenty of time. However, maybe people will say that I am a person who likes to be around girls, but I always feel that when I am close to them, a secret pain rises in my heart.

Look at this vast factory; rows and rows of seats are laid out. This is just one cigarette-packing department, and there are a thousand seats. When I ran into this brightly lit workshop, the girls who were already seated were talking and laughing. They didn't have work to do yet. This is a habit. They wait for work like this every morning. However, these more than a thousand seats now only accommodate about five hundred female workers. Moreover, they are not long-term workers. They are paid for one day's work, and they earn no more than twenty cents for a full day's work. Comparing them to me, there is a really big difference. However, I am an accountant who earns ten dollars a month, and I have to do nine hours of troublesome accounting every day. Comparing myself to those big shots who get paid for doing nothing, there is an even bigger gap. Really, every morning when I come here, I always feel a little sad.

Most of the four or five hundred girls are dressed up very nicely. I don't quite understand this. Even if they have work to do every day, working from day to night, even working a full twenty hours, they earn no more than eight or nine dollars a month. They still have to eat, so where do they get the money to look so good? Red lips, faces covered in fragrant powder, colorful clothes. Sometimes, groups of three or five gather in a corner, talking and laughing, pushing and shoving each other. Of course, if the foreman comes, they become as silent as if they were being suppressed, even furrowing their brows.

"Hey! Mr. Li, will work start today?" When I walked in, they asked me eagerly, their eyes wide with hope. Some were even eating bowls of cold rice, cold noodles, or similar things.

"Yes, someone ordered goods yesterday, so we have to rush to work today and tomorrow!"

I said, exhaling, and walked past. Their chattering voices, mixed with laughter, rose again. However, if I answered them that there was no work, they would definitely lower their heads sadly, sigh, and prepare to go home.

As usual, I finished walking through every part of the factory and returned to the office. Then, the roaring sound of the machines was continuously broadcast from every part of the factory. Five or six hundred workers were busily and quietly doing their mechanical work. As for me, wasn't I still mechanically doing my many troublesome accounts? Before, there were ten accountants, but now there are only three. Moreover, one of them is old and confused, and he often messes up the numbers and asks for help. Really, I am almost responsible for doing all the accounting work for the entire factory. You think, aren't I so busy that I can't even breathe? So, once I get to the office, my brain is no longer free.

After lunch, we heard that a worker in the baking room had fallen ill and was immediately sent to the hospital. I heard that he was suffering from scarlet fever. However, I heard a little about that worker. He was a person who drifted to Shanghai from Shandong, without relatives or friends. He came to our factory a year ago to do baking room work. This person, who was as strong as a tiger, was in the baking room, where the temperature was always above 120 degrees, breathing the suffocating smell of tobacco and hemp wine from day to night. So, he became thinner and weaker day by day, until he collapsed today. However, before long, news came from the hospital that he had indeed died of scarlet fever. Died. This terrible impression was deeply imprinted in my brain. I didn't even have the courage to walk past the door of the baking room with a temperature of over 120 degrees. However, the workers didn't make a sound, silently responding to the fact that this colleague had died for work.

"We should send some money to the worker's family as usual."

The manager mechanically asked for everyone's opinion, but many people didn't respond, remaining silent.

"Just send him five dollars!" A big shot who earned two hundred dollars a month for doing nothing said unwillingly.

Five dollars. Suppressing my grief, I recorded the number in the daily accounts. However, on the other hand, I was recording the following many numbers:

"××× banquet for official business, fifty dollars."

"××× fifty dollars, ××× car fare six dollars. ××× treat twenty-eight dollars and ninety cents!"

"×× Company demands overdue payment plus interest, totaling three thousand five hundred dollars."

"×× Bank demands interest on the mortgaged factory, twelve thousand dollars."

I sighed, but my head became dizzy and hot.

Broadcasting Script

Suzhou People (15) 203

— Gu Wenzong

Jinghong: Proving this matter, the contrast in economic power and advertising publicity is not enough, because advertising is fundamentally a means of enticing purchases. This is a necessary path for doing business and attracting customers. All those who lack economic strength will envy the colorful and beautiful sweet words on advertisements. Those beautiful and pleasant advertising terms are specifically used to swindle the money of those who have no permanent property and seek cheap things. The weaker the economic power, the more people want to enjoy various inexpensive and high-quality materials. So I say, advertising is the ultimate weapon for enticing those with weak purchasing power, and the small citizens who don't have much money and plan to get bargains are often controlled by advertising.

Liya: But isn't the greatest effect of advertising and its original intention probably more than just the base flattery you mentioned?

Jinghong: That's natural. What I said is limited to dishonest advertising. But those honest advertisements have long been forced to be powerless by those boring advertisements, deceptive advertisements, bragging advertisements, and advertisements with low-level seductive tactics! Therefore, dishonest advertising can instead deceive and control the ignorant masses.

Liya: Then the British haute cuisine I just ate must be advertising-based cuisine?

Jinghong: As long as that "British" cuisine has the effect of distinguishing flavors in your mouth, making the advertisement for that haute cuisine lose its power of deception, then you are not one of the people who have been fooled. According to what you said just now, it was so delicious, that is because the advertising's boasting has overcome the "purchaser's ability to distinguish." The purchaser has lost the "identification of matter" and the "discrimination of taste," then even the worst things become the best things.

Suzhou Ballad 205

He Yunfang, He Qinfang - Double Pearl Ball

Zhongxi (1040) 1:00 PM to 1:45 PM

Opening: "He Xiangu"

He Taiweng of Zengcheng, Guangzhou, was seventy years old and had no children, feeling disheartened. All year round, he worshipped Buddha and prayed to the gods, eating vegetarian food, burning incense, and praying to the heavens. In the spring, he offered incense everywhere, repairing temples, gilding statues, and donating generously. It has been five years now, reciting scriptures and kneeling in prayer without ceasing. His wife suddenly had a dream last night, dreaming of a five-colored phoenix entering her womb. After having the dream, within a few days, she felt a swelling in her belly that grew daily. He Taiweng knew and was overjoyed, loving the child dearly regardless of whether it was a boy or a girl. However, conceiving after a dream is quite peculiar, surely a divine gift in answer to his prayers. Time flies like water, and the months pass quickly. In an instant, ten months have passed. On the day of labor, the room was fragrant like musk, and at the time of birth, a strange red light filled the sky. The delivery was painless, and soon a baby descended from the heavens. The maid saw that it was a beautiful girl, with six strands of hair on her head, different from others. She rushed to tell He Taiweng the news, saying that the wife had safely given birth without pain, to a precious daughter. He Taiweng immediately looked at her lovely face. He Taiweng was delighted by her beautiful appearance, and his heart was filled with joy. Eighteen springs passed quickly. Xiangu was unwilling to marry a fine husband. Suddenly, in a night dream, a divine person taught her to eat mica powder. She could then lightly enter the celestial palace. From then on, she went to the mountains and valleys, walking swiftly like the wind. Later, Wu Dun learned of her and summoned her. While traveling through Guanzhong, she suddenly disappeared. Later, she ascended to heaven in broad daylight and entered the Ziwei Palace.

Movies

MGM Produced "Romeo and Juliet" 209

— Zhen

A year ago, Warner Bros.' "A Midsummer Night's Dream" was completed. Originally, other Hollywood companies were secretly preparing to produce a large number of Shakespearean plays, but due to Warner's failure, they all abandoned their plans.

MGM, which has always been known for its bold investments, was not daunted by this. They were still unwilling to abandon this new path that could be opened up. So they decided to produce a film of "Romeo and Juliet."

According to estimates, the cost of this film will reach US$1.25 million.

The producer paid special attention to the dialogue in Shakespeare's original work. In order to be precise and accurate, they searched through eighteen different versions. Finally, it was decided to use the Cambridge edition of the original book.

Also, in order to accurately understand the situation of the city of Verona in the 1400s, the film's art director, Mr. Gibbons, sent two photographers to this ancient Italian city to observe. They spent three months there, taking 3,769 related photos, from which they made dozens of scale models, and then built magnificent studio sets based on the models.

A set of Verona's central square alone covered eight acres. Another large ballroom was 250 feet wide across the ends and 400 feet long. Capulet's garden was also the same size, but it looked even wider than the ballroom. The balcony, which Romeo had to climb up with its roots covered in roses (one of the most intoxicating scenes in the original), was 24 feet high.

The biggest expense of this film was still on the actors' costumes. The film had more than 1,200 male and female actors, and the female costumes were much more troublesome than the male ones; they used 20,000 yards of silk, while the males used 18,000 yards. Romeo's jacket alone used nine yards, but Leslie Howard wore it four times, so it was worth it in the end.

"Romeo and Juliet," starring Norma Shearer as Juliet, will be released soon in this city. It is the second Shakespearean film adaptation in the last two years. In total, Hollywood has paid nearly three million gold yuan for Shakespeare on these two films.
